Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner Sagora Senior Living contact form
URLhttps://www.sagora.com/contact/
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score984
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 984, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 155. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 8. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 106

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test link-name, score 30 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 40 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.EmptyNoId, score 4 (Link has no name or id attribute or value)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.NoContent, score 40 (Link has an href attribute but no text)
  • Package wave, test e:link_empty, score 40 (Link contains no text)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 40 (Link has no text inside it)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 63

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 26 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 51 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 50

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 48 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 50

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 48 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)
